<hr style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'/><p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><b>Item 5.07. Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders</b></p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0'>On April 26, 2022, Associated Banc-Corp (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) conducted its 2022 Annual Meeting of Shareholders. &#160;The results of the matters submitted to a shareholder vote at the Annual Meeting were as follows:</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0;color:#000000'>&#160;</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin:0'><b>(1) Election of the below-named nominees to the Board of Directors of the Company:</b></p>

<P style='font:16pt Arial;margin:0'><KBD style='position:absolute;text-align:right;font:16pt Times New Roman;width:490.5pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000'></KBD>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:16pt Arial;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P align=center style='font:16pt Arial;margin:0'><B>Associated Announces Annual Meeting Results and Dividends</B></P>
<P align=center style='font:16pt Franklin Gothic Demi;margin:0'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><B>GREEN BAY, Wis. </B>&#8211;&#8211; April 26, 2022 &#8211;&#8211; Associated Banc-Corp (NYSE:ASB) (&#8220;Associated&#8221;) today announced the results of the actions taken at its 2022 Annual Meeting of Shareholders.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'>The following directors were re-elected:</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>John (Jay) B. Williams, chairman, Associated Banc-Corp, and chairman, Church Mutual&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-left:36pt;margin-right:-2.7pt'>Insurance Company</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Andrew J. Harmening, president and chief executive officer, Associated Banc-Corp&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>R. Jay Gerken, director of 17 mutual funds associated with Sanford C. Bernstein Fund, Inc.&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Judith P. Greffin, former chief investment officer, Allstate Corporation&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-right:-7.9pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Michael J. Haddad, chair of the board of directors, Schreiber Foods, Inc.&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Robert A. Jeffe, senior operating partner, BlackWatch&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Eileen A. Kamerick, adjunct professor of law and consultant&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Gale E. Klappa, executive chairman, WEC Energy Group&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Cory L. Nettles, founder and managing director, Generation Growth Capital, Inc.&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'><KBD style='position:absolute;font:10pt Arial;margin-left:0pt'>&#45;</KBD><KBD style=margin-left:36pt></KBD>Karen T. van Lith, founder and CEO of APEL Worldwide, LLC&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-right:-8.1pt'>Shareholders also (1) gave advisory approval to named executive officer compensation, and (2) ratified the selection of KPMG LLP as Associated&#8217;s independent accounting firm for 2022.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>The Associated Board of Directors declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.20 per common share, payable on June&#160;15, 2022, to shareholders of record at the close of business on June 1, 2022. </P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'>The Board of Directors also declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.3671875 per depositary share on Associated&#8217;s 5.875% Series E Perpetual Preferred Stock, payable on June 15, 2022, to shareholders of record at the close of business on June 1, 2022.</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0'>The Board of Directors also declared a regular quarterly cash dividend of $0.3515625 per depositary share on Associated&#8217;s 5.625% Series F Perpetual Preferred Stock, payable on June 15, 2022, to shareholders of record at the close of business on June 1, 2022.</P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><HR style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'><P style=line-height:0;margin:0></P>
<HR style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'><P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-right:-7.9pt;background-color:#FFFFFF'><B>ABOUT ASSOCIATED BANC-CORP</B></P>
<P align=justify style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:6pt;margin-bottom:15pt'>Associated Banc-Corp (NYSE: ASB) has total assets of $35 billion and is Wisconsin's largest bank holding company.&#160;Headquartered in Green Bay, Wisconsin, Associated is a leading Midwest banking franchise, offering a full range of financial products and services from more than 200 banking locations serving more than 100 communities throughout Wisconsin, Illinois and Minnesota. The company also operates loan production offices in Indiana, Michigan, Missouri, New York, Ohio and Texas. Associated Bank, N.A. is an Equal Housing Lender, Equal Opportunity Lender and Member FDIC. More information about Associated Banc-Corp is available at <FONT style='color:#0000FF;border-bottom:1px solid #0000FF'>www.associatedbank.com</FONT>.</P>
<P align=center style='font:10pt Arial;margin:0;margin-right:-7.9pt;background-color:#FFFFFF'>&nbsp;</P>
<P style='font:10pt Arial;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:6pt;margin-right:-7.9pt;background-color:#FFFFFF'><B>FORWARD LOOKING STATEMENTS</B></P>

This includes any statements regarding management&#8217;s plans, objectives, or goals for future operations, products or services, and forecasts of its revenues, earnings, or other measures of performance.&#160;Such forward-looking statements may be identified by the use of words such as &#8220;believe,&#8221; &#8220;expect,&#8221; &#8220;anticipate,&#8221; &#8220;plan,&#8221; &#8220;estimate,&#8221; &#8220;should,&#8221; &#8220;will,&#8221; &#8220;intend,&#8221; &quot;target,&quot; &#8220;outlook,&#8221; &#8220;project,&#8221; &quot;guidance,&quot;</I> <I>or similar expressions.&#160;Forward-looking statements are based on current management expectations and, by their nature, are subject to risks and uncertainties. Actual results may differ materially from those contained in the forward-looking statements.&#160;Factors which may cause actual results to differ materially from those contained in such forward-looking statements include those identified in the Company&#8217;s most recent Form 10-K and subsequent SEC filings.&#160;Such factors are incorporated herein by reference.&#160;</I></P>
